        )

                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) = LOWER(:exact) THEN 1
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:startsWith) THEN 2
                ELSE 3 
            END,
            asset_name 
        LIMIT 10

            asset_name,

            department
        FROM request_table

            LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(reg_no) LIKE LOWER(:search)

        )

                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:startsWith) THEN 2
                ELSE 3 
            END,
            asset_name 
        LIMIT 10

            asset_name,
            reg_no,
            category,
            CAST(quantity AS SIGNED) as quantity,
            department
        FROM request_table
        WHERE (
            LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(reg_no) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(category) LIKE LOWER(:search)
        )
        AND asset_name IS NOT NULL
        AND quantity > 0
        ORDER BY 
            CASE 
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) = LOWER(:exact) THEN 1
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:startsWith) THEN 2
                ELSE 3 
            END,
            asset_name 
        LIMIT 10

            reg_no,
            category,
            CAST(quantity AS SIGNED) as quantity,
            department
        FROM request_table

            LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(reg_no) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(category) LIKE LOWER(:search)
        )
        AND asset_name IS NOT NULL
        AND quantity > 0
        ORDER BY 
            CASE 
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) = LOWER(:exact) THEN 1
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:startsWith) THEN 2
                ELSE 3 
            END,
            asset_name 
        LIMIT 10

            reg_no,
            category,
            CAST(quantity AS SIGNED) as quantity,
            department
        FROM request_table
        WHERE (
            LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(reg_no) LIKE LOWER(:search)
            OR LOWER(category) LIKE LOWER(:search)
        )
        AND asset_name IS NOT NULL
        AND quantity > 0
        ORDER BY 
            CASE 
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) = LOWER(:exact) THEN 1
                WHEN LOWER(asset_name) LIKE LOWER(:startsWith) THEN 2
                ELSE 3 
            END,
            asset_name 
        LIMIT 10
